metadata\\n\\n### Summary of Key Components\\n\\n1. **Entry**: HTTP handler receives JSON request at `/apis/*/datasources/{uid}/query`\\n2. **Routing**: PluginHandler routes to QueryDataHandler which Kubernetes TypeMeta and serialized to JSON via Responder\\n7. **Output**: HTTP response contains JSON representation of the data frames with all field metadata\\n\\nThe entire flow uses the Grafana
